    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText1572353044394202412" style="display:none">Wtf did I just read?<br />First of all, I am not a scientist or a doctor and I cannot and will not make any judgment as to validity of author's claims. <div id="review_3579754144" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3579754144" />
    <a title="Susan Da Silva" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/122412099-susan-da-silva"><img alt="Susan Da Silva" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602332896p2/122412099.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3579754144?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan Da Silva" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan Da Silva" href="/user/show/122412099-susan-da-silva">Susan Da Silva</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3579754144" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6922183928483939209">A relief to finally read a book written about cancer and other diseases which doesn't tout unproven cures but instead explains the cause of these diseases. It doesn't take rocket science to figure out that what we need to cure diseases is an explanation of their cause that agrees with facts. I wonder why I have not heard about this theory in the news until now when it also explains facts that have been observed during epidemics and pandemics which the germ theory cannot explain and therefore sho</span>
  <span id="freeText6922183928483939209" style="display:none">A relief to finally read a book written about cancer and other diseases which doesn't tout unproven cures but instead explains the cause of these diseases. It doesn't take rocket science to figure out that what we need to cure diseases is an explanation of their cause that agrees with facts. I wonder why I have not heard about this theory in the news until now when it also explains facts that have been observed during epidemics and pandemics which the germ theory cannot explain and therefore should be the most talked about theory in the world right now. His theory explains facts which are beyond the reach of the most famous theories, from Darwin's theory of evolution to the germ theory. <br /><br />This is the most revolutionary theory since Einstein's relativity. It's mind-blowing. Germs become essential for the production of certain manifestations by diseases but not their cause! Diseases appear at beginning of life which the aging concept describes as a period of health! As though that were not enough, evolution becomes a process by which organisms of different origin have changed to delay death from diseases in ways that have made them more similar since they became exposed to the cause of diseases at some point in their history and the similarities between organisms of different kinds no longer represent origin from a single common ancestor as Darwin proposed them to be! As a person of faith, I am super happy that science finally has a theory of evolution that creationists like me can finally accept because it is justifiable. This is a book that everyone should read and I am so surprised that a theory of science could be made so simple and enjoyable. The value of this book is far beyond the price!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6922183928483939209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yefuE9R36uCreJhe7ntfKO63YYFoAj1l3WybNGQxrE0pUyuTCr5bxKjY6uYnqsomEFp7Fk39te7i7QpjAJSUTQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RXLDX2rDmbLo/+Kx96wnTRC1lK0GuJsrMIsAGZEGfxSlxgbftAoolutfkAk+fbJD7liOOiNHE6APCpFO9aNHFA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Cosmos traces the origins of knowledge and the scientific method, mixing science and philosophy, and speculates to the future of science. You don\'t have to.   Award-winning author Janice Hardy (and founder of the popular writing site, Fiction University) takes you deep into one of the most frustrating aspects of writing--showing, and not telling. <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText3385038467265204187\" style=\"display:none\">Do you struggle with show, don\'t tell? You don\'t have to.   Award-winning author Janice Hardy (and founder of the popular writing site, Fiction University) takes you deep into one of the most frustrating aspects of writing--showing, and not telling. She\'ll help you understand what show, don\'t tell means, teach you how to spot told prose in your writing, and reveal why common advice on how to fix it doesn\'t always work.  With in-depth analysis, \n  Understanding Show, Don\'t Tell (And Really Getting It)\n looks at what affects told prose and when telling is the right thing to do. It also explores aspects of writing that aren’t technically telling, but are connected to told prose and can make prose feel told, such as infodumps, description, and backstory.  Her easy-to-understand examples will show you clear before and after text and demonstrate how telling words change the prose. You\'ll learn how to find the right balance between description, narrative, and internalization for the strongest impact. These examples will also demonstrate why showing the wrong details can sound just as dull as telling.  This book will help you:  Understand when to tell and when to show Spot common red flag words often found in told prose Learn why one single rule doesn\'t apply to all books Determine how much telling is acceptable in your writing Fix stale or flat prose holding your writing back  \n  Understanding Show, Don\'t Tell (And Really Getting It)\n is more than just advice on what to do and what not to do—it’s a down and dirty examination and analysis of how show, don’t tell works, so you can adapt the “rules” to whatever style or genre you’re writing. By the end of this book, you’ll have a solid understanding of show, don’t tell and the ability to use it without fear or frustration.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"3385038467265204187\" href=\"#\" Even after more than three centuries and the revolutions of Einsteinian relativity and quantum mechanics, Newtonian physics continues to account for many of the phenomena of the observed world, and Newtonian celestial dynamics is used to determine the orbits of our space vehicles.This completely new translation, the first in 270 years, is based on the third (1726) edition, the final revised version approved by Newton; it includes extracts from the earlier editions, corrects errors found in earlier versions, and replaces archaic English with contemporary prose and up-to-date mathematical forms. Newton\'s principles describe acceleration, deceleration, and inertial movement; fluid dynamics; and the motions of the earth, moon, planets, and comets. A great work in itself, the Principia also revolutionized the methods of scientific investigation. It set forth the fundamental three laws of motion and the law of universal gravity, the physical principles that account for the Copernican system of the world as emended by Kepler, thus effectively ending controversy concerning the Copernican planetary system.The illuminating Guide to the Principia by I. November 2015 is the 100th anniversary of Einstein’s discovery of the General Theory of Relativity.\n\nLevenson, head of MIT’s Science Writing Program, tells the captivating, unusual, and nearly-forgotten backstory behind Einstein’s invention of the Theory of Relativity, which completely changed the course of science forever. For over 50 years before Einstein developed his theory, the world’s top astronomers spent countless hours and energy searching for a planet, which came to be named Vulcan, that had to exist, it was thought, given Isaac Newton’s theories of gravity. Indeed, in the two centuries since Newton’s death, his theory had essentially become accepted as fact. It took Einstein’s genius to realize the mystery of the missing planet wasn’t a problem of measurements or math but of Newton’s theory of gravity itself. Einstein’s Theory of Relativity proved that Vulcan did not and could not exist, and that the decades-long search for it had merely been a quirk of operating under the wrong set of assumptions about the universe. Thomas Levenson tells this unique story, one of the strangest episodes in the history of science, with elegant simplicity, fast-paced drama, and lively characters sure to capture the attention of a       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/20609623.Paul_Ola">About Paul Ola</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/20609623.Paul_Ola"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1602545618p3/20609623.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14430147732060603655">As a child, Paul Ola was inspired by the story of the most famous theorist of science, Albert Einstein who, in the early 1900s, when he was only a clerk at the Swiss patent office in Bern, developed groundbreaking explanations that enabled scientists to solve problems which were beyond the capacity of the explanations that Sir Isaac Newton, the University of Cambridge professor and great father of</span>
  <span id="freeText14430147732060603655" style="display:none">As a child, Paul Ola was inspired by the story of the most famous theorist of science, Albert Einstein who, in the early 1900s, when he was only a clerk at the Swiss patent office in Bern, developed groundbreaking explanations that enabled scientists to solve problems which were beyond the capacity of the explanations that Sir Isaac Newton, the University of Cambridge professor and great father of the field of science that is known as physics, published in 1687 despite the adjustments that the most highly respected theorists in universities made to these explanations in the century of Einstein's birth.<br /><br />So great were the contributions of the explanations of this most famous of clerks to the capacity of scientists to solve problems that he was awarded a PhD by the University of Zurich, employed by universities as a theoretical physicist (a theorist who explains things that are of doubtful causes or nature in the field of physics) and appointed a professor. And for these great contributions, Einstein was awarded that most prestigious of prizes that is known as the Nobel prize in 1921 for his services to Theoretical physics.<br /><br />When Ola found at the beginning of his studies at the University of Ibadan (which Africa’s first Nobel Laureate, Professor Wole Soyinka attended decades before him) that the cause of the rise of the likelihood of being killed by the ultimate manifestations of diseases as age increases remained unknown despite over a century of intensive research at the institutes in our greatest universities as well as those that are outside of them, he knew that the true cause of any of these diseases, which include those such as COVID-19 that the germ theory proposed to be caused essentially and solely by infectious or spreading agents, could not be known until the cause of this fact became known.<br /><br />And he realized that just like the explanations that Einstein formed to solve problems that Newton's explanations could not, the explanations that must be formed to solve problems of biology and medicine that are connected with the inability to explain the cause of the long known association between age and the likelihood of being killed by the ultimate manifestations of diseases, most important among which is our inability to cure these manifestations, could only be developed by a theorist with the opportunity to work in an environment like the Swiss patent office of Einstein's day and access to the time and opportunity required to think about problems in a new way until they are solved.<br /><br />Therefore, when he found that none of the established career ladders at our universities and their research institutes for which he was qualified would give him the time and opportunity that he needed to think about the longstanding problems of biology and medicine in a new way as Einstein thought about the longstanding problems of physics to solve them, he searched for these explanations at the expense of the climb to the peak of these ladders and the steadily growing income that accompanies such a climb.<br /><br />He formed a new concept that described the unknown cause of the association between age and the likelihood of being killed by diseases as a factor which brings cancers and other chronic diseases into existence in our bodies at the beginning of life, long before we are exposed to advancing age, infectious or spreading agents and other factors to which the deadly manifestations of these chronic diseases were attributed in the absence of this concept and he referred to this factor as their "root cause" since, upon its removal from our bodies, these diseases would disappear along with their deadly ultimate manifestations despite the fact that we cannot remove factors that include infectious agents such as viruses which we believed to be the cause of such manifestations in the absence of this concept. <br /><br />After enduring...There is not enough room for Paul Ola's biography here, you can read more at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amazon.com/author/paulola">https://www.amazon.com/author/paulola</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14430147732060603655" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
